          --monorail-metadata-toggled-bg: var(--monorail-metadata-closed-bg);
        }
        mr-issue-page[codeFont] {
          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;
        }

          flex-grow: 1;

          flex-wrap: no-wrap;

        }

          width: 100%;

          top: var(--monorail-header-height);
          height: calc(100vh - var(--monorail-header-height));
        }

            width: 100%;

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

Steps to reproduce the problem:



<b class="line"><!---->Steps to reproduce the problem:<!----></b>



<br>





commit 



<span class="line"><!---->commit <!----></span>





d5e65e8f5f8f26bea38c82c2ee72f11e1af5b6f4



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crrev.com/d5e65e8f5f8f26bea38c82c2ee72f11e1af5b6f4"><!---->d5e65e8f5f8f26bea38c82c2ee72f11e1af5b6f4<!----></a>



<br>





1. apply the change.txt and compile chrome with ASAN



<span class="line"><!---->1. apply the change.txt and compile chrome with ASAN<!----></span>



<br>





2. `python copy_mojo_js_bindings.py path/to/ASAN/gen/` and copy poc.html to the same folder



<span class="line"><!---->2. `python copy_mojo_js_bindings.py path/to/ASAN/gen/` and copy poc.html to the same folder<!----></span>



<br>





3. start a server at poc.html's folder : python -m SimpleHTTPServer 8605



<span class="line"><!---->3. start a server at poc.html's folder : python -m SimpleHTTPServer 8605<!----></span>



<br>





4. ASAN/chrome --enable-blink-features=MojoJS --user-data-dir=/tmp/noexist 



<span class="line"><!---->4. ASAN/chrome --enable-blink-features=MojoJS --user-data-dir=/tmp/noexist <!----></span>





http://127.0.0.1:8605/poc.html



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="http://127.0.0.1:8605/poc.html"><!---->http://127.0.0.1:8605/poc.html<!----></a>



<br>





5. click submit button and save the password, then close the popup 



<span class="line"><!---->5. click submit button and save the password, then close the popup <!----></span>



<br>





6. input any text, submit and then save the password again



<span class="line"><!---->6. input any text, submit and then save the password again<!----></span>



<br>





7. if this doesn't crash the browser, repeat setp6 again



<span class="line"><!---->7. if this doesn't crash the browser, repeat setp6 again<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Problem Description:



<b class="line"><!---->Problem Description:<!----></b>



<br>





This is found by fuzzing, I'm not familiar with this code, and don't figure out the root cause of this problem. So the analysis maybe not right :P



<span class="line"><!---->This is found by fuzzing, I'm not familiar with this code, and don't figure out the root cause of this problem. So the analysis maybe not right :P<!----></span>



<br>





The patch is used to simulate the leak of passwords.



<span class="line"><!---->The patch is used to simulate the leak of passwords.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>





When we save a leaked password, it will be stored in `std::vector<const PasswordForm*> insecure_credentials_` of class `FormFetcherImpl`[1].



<span class="line"><!---->When we save a leaked password, it will be stored in `std::vector&lt;const PasswordForm*&gt; insecure_credentials_` of class `FormFetcherImpl`[1].<!----></span>



<br>





The Mojo `credential.store` will call `client_->NotifyStorePasswordCalled` [2], which will reset the `FormManager` and destruct the `FormFetcherImpl`, and the `PasswordForm` strore in `FomFetcherImpl` will also be reset.



<span class="line"><!---->The Mojo `credential.store` will call `client_-&gt;NotifyStorePasswordCalled` [2], which will reset the `FormManager` and destruct the `FormFetcherImpl`, and the `PasswordForm` strore in `FomFetcherImpl` will also be reset.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

After some debug, I think I have found the root cause of this issue.



<span class="line"><!---->After some debug, I think I have found the root cause of this issue.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





`FormFetcherImpl::Clone()` will copy `FormFetcherImpl` to make a new unique_ptr[1]. The copy of unique_ptr is implemented by `MakeCopies`[2], it will create a new unique_ptr use the origin unique_ptr's raw ptr. This is OK, but the raw_ptr is copied directly, which should be the new unique_ptr's raw ptr, rather than the origin raw ptr.



<span class="line"><!---->`FormFetcherImpl::Clone()` will copy `FormFetcherImpl` to make a new unique_ptr[1]. The copy of unique_ptr is implemented by `MakeCopies`[2], it will create a new unique_ptr use the origin unique_ptr's raw ptr. This is OK, but the raw_ptr is copied directly, which should be the new unique_ptr's raw ptr, rather than the origin raw ptr.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





```[1]



<span class="line"><!---->```[1]<!----></span>



<br>





std::unique_ptr<FormFetcher> FormFetcherImpl::Clone() {



<span class="line"><!---->std::unique_ptr&lt;FormFetcher&gt; FormFetcherImpl::Clone() {<!----></span>



<br>





  // Create the copy without the "HTTPS migration" activated. If it was needed,



<span class="line"><!---->  // Create the copy without the "HTTPS migration" activated. If it was needed,<!----></span>



<br>





  // then it was done by |this| already.



<span class="line"><!---->  // then it was done by |this| already.<!----></span>



<br>





  auto result = std::make_unique<FormFetcherImpl>(form_digest_, client_, false);



<span class="line"><!---->  auto result = std::make_unique&lt;FormFetcherImpl&gt;(form_digest_, client_, false);<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





  if (state_ != State::NOT_WAITING) {



<span class="line"><!---->  if (state_ != State::NOT_WAITING) {<!----></span>



<br>





    // There are no store results to copy, trigger a Fetch on the clone instead.



<span class="line"><!---->    // There are no store results to copy, trigger a Fetch on the clone instead.<!----></span>



<br>





    result->Fetch();



<span class="line"><!---->    result-&gt;Fetch();<!----></span>



<br>





    return result;



<span class="line"><!---->    return result;<!----></span>



<br>





  }



<span class="line"><!---->  }<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





  result->non_federated_ = MakeCopies(non_federated_);



<span class="line"><!---->  result-&gt;non_federated_ = MakeCopies(non_federated_);<!----></span>



<br>





  result->federated_ = MakeCopies(federated_);



<span class="line"><!---->  result-&gt;federated_ = MakeCopies(federated_);<!----></span>



<br>





  result->is_blocklisted_in_account_store_ = is_blocklisted_in_account_store_;



<span class="line"><!---->  result-&gt;is_blocklisted_in_account_store_ = is_blocklisted_in_account_store_;<!----></span>



<br>





  result->is_blocklisted_in_profile_store_ = is_blocklisted_in_profile_store_;



<span class="line"><!---->  result-&gt;is_blocklisted_in_profile_store_ = is_blocklisted_in_profile_store_;<!----></span>



<br>





  password_manager_util::FindBestMatches(



<span class="line"><!---->  password_manager_util::FindBestMatches(<!----></span>



<br>





      MakeWeakCopies(result->non_federated_), form_digest_.scheme,



<span class="line"><!---->      MakeWeakCopies(result-&gt;non_federated_), form_digest_.scheme,<!----></span>



<br>





      &result->non_federated_same_scheme_, &result->best_matches_,



<span class="line"><!---->      &amp;result-&gt;non_federated_same_scheme_, &amp;result-&gt;best_matches_,<!----></span>



<br>





      &result->preferred_match_);



<span class="line"><!---->      &amp;result-&gt;preferred_match_);<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





  result->interactions_stats_ = interactions_stats_;



<span class="line"><!---->  result-&gt;interactions_stats_ = interactions_stats_;<!----></span>



<br>





  result->insecure_credentials_ = insecure_credentials_;



<span class="line"><!---->  result-&gt;insecure_credentials_ = insecure_credentials_;<!----></span>



<br>





  result->state_ = state_;



<span class="line"><!---->  result-&gt;state_ = state_;<!----></span>



<br>





  result->need_to_refetch_ = need_to_refetch_;



<span class="line"><!---->  result-&gt;need_to_refetch_ = need_to_refetch_;<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





  return result;



<span class="line"><!---->  return result;<!----></span>



<br>





}



<span class="line"><!---->}<!----></span>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





```[2]



<span class="line"><!---->```[2]<!----></span>



<br>





std::vector<std::unique_ptr<PasswordForm>> MakeCopies(



<span class="line"><!---->std::vector&lt;std::unique_ptr&lt;PasswordForm&gt;&gt; MakeCopies(<!----></span>



<br>





    const std::vector<std::unique_ptr<PasswordForm>>& source) {



<span class="line"><!---->    const std::vector&lt;std::unique_ptr&lt;PasswordForm&gt;&gt;&amp; source) {<!----></span>



<br>





  std::vector<std::unique_ptr<PasswordForm>> result(source.size());



<span class="line"><!---->  std::vector&lt;std::unique_ptr&lt;PasswordForm&gt;&gt; result(source.size());<!----></span>



<br>





  std::transform(source.begin(), source.end(), result.begin(),



<span class="line"><!---->  std::transform(source.begin(), source.end(), result.begin(),<!----></span>



<br>





                 [](const std::unique_ptr<PasswordForm>& ptr) {



<span class="line"><!---->                 [](const std::unique_ptr&lt;PasswordForm&gt;&amp; ptr) {<!----></span>



<br>





                   return std::make_unique<PasswordForm>(*ptr);



<span class="line"><!---->                   return std::make_unique&lt;PasswordForm&gt;(*ptr);<!----></span>



<br>





                 });



<span class="line"><!---->                 });<!----></span>



<br>





  return result;



<span class="line"><!---->  return result;<!----></span>



<br>





}



<span class="line"><!---->}<!----></span>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Therefore we can patch this issue by assigning the right value to raw ptr `insecure_credentials_`.



<span class="line"><!---->Therefore we can patch this issue by assigning the right value to raw ptr `insecure_credentials_`.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





example patch:



<span class="line"><!---->example patch:<!----></span>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>





diff --git a/components/password_manager/core/browser/form_fetcher_impl.cc b/components/password_manager/core/browser/form_fetcher_impl.cc



<span class="line"><!---->diff --git a/components/password_manager/core/browser/form_fetcher_impl.cc b/components/password_manager/core/browser/form_fetcher_impl.cc<!----></span>



<br>





index 2a5e507b6366..19d396124485 100644



<span class="line"><!---->index 2a5e507b6366..19d396124485 100644<!----></span>



<br>





--- a/components/password_manager/core/browser/form_fetcher_impl.cc



<span class="line"><!---->--- a/components/password_manager/core/browser/form_fetcher_impl.cc<!----></span>



<br>





+++ b/components/password_manager/core/browser/form_fetcher_impl.cc



<span class="line"><!---->+++ b/components/password_manager/core/browser/form_fetcher_impl.cc<!----></span>



<br>





@@ -230,7 +230,15 @@ std::unique_ptr<FormFetcher> FormFetcherImpl::Clone() {



<span class="line"><!---->@@ -230,7 +230,15 @@ std::unique_ptr&lt;FormFetcher&gt; FormFetcherImpl::Clone() {<!----></span>



<br>





       &result->preferred_match_);



<span class="line"><!---->       &amp;result-&gt;preferred_match_);<!----></span>



<br>





 



<span class="line"><!----> <!----></span>



<br>





   result->interactions_stats_ = interactions_stats_;



<span class="line"><!---->   result-&gt;interactions_stats_ = interactions_stats_;<!----></span>



<br>





-  result->insecure_credentials_ = insecure_credentials_;



<span class="line"><!---->-  result-&gt;insecure_credentials_ = insecure_credentials_;<!----></span>



<br>





+  //result->insecure_credentials_ = insecure_credentials_;



<span class="line"><!---->+  //result-&gt;insecure_credentials_ = insecure_credentials_;<!----></span>



<br>





+  for (auto& form : result->federated_) {



<span class="line"><!---->+  for (auto&amp; form : result-&gt;federated_) {<!----></span>



<br>





+    if (!form->password_issues.empty())



<span class="line"><!---->+    if (!form-&gt;password_issues.empty())<!----></span>



<br>





+        result->insecure_credentials_.push_back(form.get());



<span class="line"><!---->+        result-&gt;insecure_credentials_.push_back(form.get());<!----></span>



<br>





+  }



<span class="line"><!---->+  }<!----></span>



<br>





+  for (auto& form : result->non_federated_) {



<span class="line"><!---->+  for (auto&amp; form : result-&gt;non_federated_) {<!----></span>



<br>





+    if (!form->password_issues.empty())



<span class="line"><!---->+    if (!form-&gt;password_issues.empty())<!----></span>



<br>





+        result->insecure_credentials_.push_back(form.get());



<span class="line"><!---->+        result-&gt;insecure_credentials_.push_back(form.get());<!----></span>



<br>





+  }



<span class="line"><!---->+  }<!----></span>



<br>





   result->state_ = state_;



<span class="line"><!---->   result-&gt;state_ = state_;<!----></span>



<br>





   result->need_to_refetch_ = need_to_refetch_;



<span class="line"><!---->   result-&gt;need_to_refetch_ = need_to_refetch_;<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





```

performant, it reduces the risk of those pointers going stale during

<br>





future refactorings.

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

           * there's spacing. */

        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container td {
          padding: 0.25em 8px;
          white-space: nowrap;
        }
        .screenreader-hidden {
          clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);
          height: 1px;
          overflow: hidden;
          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;
        }
      </style>
      <div class="chops-autocomplete-container">
        <span class="screenreader-hidden" aria-live="polite">
          
        </span>
        <table hidden="">
          <tbody>
            
          </tbody>
        </table>
      </div>
    <!----></mr-autocomplete>
            </div>
          </div>

      <style>
        mr-issue-page {

 runOnLoad(function() {

 let cl = new ClientLogger("issues");
 if (cl.started("new-issue")) {
 cl.logEnd("new-issue", null, 120 * 1000);
 }
 if (cl.started("issue-search")) {
 cl.logEnd("issue-search");
 }
 }
 });
